645     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < \hyperlink{lev__main_8c_a45e1d3556bb40a075f6665d5f896a28f}{nrooms}; i++)
646         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{lev__main_8c_af394e9350936ef56f1ec921a8abe60eb}{tmproom}[i]->parent) \{
647         n\_subrooms = 0;
648         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(j = i; j < \hyperlink{lev__main_8c_a45e1d3556bb40a075f6665d5f896a28f}{nrooms}; j++) \{
649 \textcolor{comment}{/*}
650 \textcolor{comment}{ *  This is by no means perfect, but should cut down the duplicate error}
651 \textcolor{comment}{ *  messages by over 90%.  The only problem will be when either subrooms}
652 \textcolor{comment}{ *  are mixed in the level definition (not likely but possible) or rooms}
653 \textcolor{comment}{ *  have subrooms that have subrooms.}
654 \textcolor{comment}{ */}
655             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!strcmp(\hyperlink{lev__main_8c_af394e9350936ef56f1ec921a8abe60eb}{tmproom}[i]->parent, last\_parent)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};
656             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{lev__main_8c_af394e9350936ef56f1ec921a8abe60eb}{tmproom}[j]->parent &&
657                 !strcmp(\hyperlink{lev__main_8c_af394e9350936ef56f1ec921a8abe60eb}{tmproom}[i]->parent, \hyperlink{lev__main_8c_af394e9350936ef56f1ec921a8abe60eb}{tmproom}[j]->parent)) \{
658             n\_subrooms++;
659             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(n\_subrooms > \hyperlink{global_8h_a434176f3fe018fa4c6ba570d8fe36b14}{MAX\_SUBROOMS}) \{
660 
661                 \hyperlink{global_8h_aa55ba8f4e3c82fe00035e6b51d6c7dee}{Sprintf}(msg,
662           \textcolor{stringliteral}{"Subroom error: too many subrooms attached to parent room '%s'!"},
663                     \hyperlink{lev__main_8c_af394e9350936ef56f1ec921a8abe60eb}{tmproom}[i]->parent);
664                 \hyperlink{lev__main_8c_a93d4cdd711598f90c5c453a60c2d0ddf}{yyerror}(msg);
665                 last\_parent = \hyperlink{lev__main_8c_af394e9350936ef56f1ec921a8abe60eb}{tmproom}[i]->\hyperlink{struct__room_ad0c17b49155ae5f1517fa3227e0d48e6}{parent};
666                 ok = \hyperlink{global_8h_aa93f0eb578d23995850d61f7d61c55c1}{FALSE};
667                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
668             \}
669             \}
670         \}
671         \}
672     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ok;
673 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
